<h1 class="article-title" style="margin:0px; padding:0px 0px 16px; border-width:0px 0px 2px; border-top-style:initial; border-right-style:initial; border-bottom-style:solid; border-left-style:initial; border-top-color:initial; border-right-color:initial; border-bottom-color:rgb(221,221,221); border-left-color:initial; outline:0px; font-style:inherit; font-family:inherit; vertical-align:baseline; line-height:1.1em">
Kafka和Spring集成实践</h1>
<div class="article-entry" style='margin:0px; padding:0px 20px; border:0px; outline:0px; font-family:"Helvetica Neue",Helvetica,Arial,sans-serif; font-size:16px; vertical-align:baseline; zoom:1; counter-reset:section 0 subsection 0'>
<h1 id="expanderHead" style='margin:0px 0px 2em; padding:0.1em 0.3em; border-top:0px; border-right:0px; border-bottom:none; border-left:0px; outline:0px; font-style:inherit; font-family:"Droid Serif","Segoe UI",Georgia,serif; font-size:1.2em; vertical-align:baseline; line-height:1.1em'>
目录 <span id="expanderSign" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; border:0px; outline:0px; font-weight:inherit; font-style:inherit; font-family:inherit; font-size:0.5em; vertical-align:middle; line-height:1.1em">[−]</span></h1>

<a target="_blank" class="toc-link" href="http://www.colobu.com/2014/11/19/kafka-spring-integration-in-practice/#%E4%BD%BF%E7%94%A8spring-integration-kafka%E6%8E%A5%E6%94%B6%E6%B6%88%E6%81%AF" rel="nofollow" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; border:0px; outline:0px; font-weight:inherit; font-style:inherit; font-family:inherit; vertical-align:baseline; color:rgb(227,45,64); text-decoration:none">使用spring-integration-kafka接收消息</a></li></ol>
</li></ol>
</div>
<p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:20px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; border:0px; outline:0px; font-weight:inherit; font-style:inherit; font-family:inherit; vertical-align:baseline; letter-spacing:0.01rem; line-height:2em">
本文以单机的环境演示如何将Kafka和Spring集成。<br>
单机的环境最容易搭建， 并且只需在自己的PC上运行即可， 不需要很多的硬件环境，便于学习。 况且，本文的目的不是搭建ZooKeeper的集群环境， 而是重点介绍Kafka和Spring的应用。<br>
具体的软件环境如下：</p>
<ul style="margin:0.8em 20px; padding:0px; border:0px; outline:0px; font-weight:inherit; font-style:inherit; font-family:inherit; vertical-align:baseline; list-style-position:initial; line-height:1.6em; counter-reset:item 0">
<li style="margin:0px; padding:0px; border:0px; outline:0px; font-weight:inherit; font-style:inherit; font-family:inherit; vertical-align:baseline">
OS: CentOS 6.4</li><li style="margin:0px; padding:0px; border:0px; outline:0px; font-weight:inherit; font-style:inherit; font-family:inherit; vertical-align:baseline">
Zookepper： zookeeper-3.4.6</li><li style="margin:0px; padding:0px; border:0px; outline:0px; font-weight:inherit; font-style:inherit; font-family:inherit; vertical-align:baseline">
Kafka： kafka_2.9.1-0.8.2-beta</li><li style="margin:0px; padding:0px; border:0px; outline:0px; font-weight:inherit; font-style:inherit; font-family:inherit; vertical-align:baseline">
Java： JDK 1.7.0_45-b18</li><li style="margin:0px; padding:0px; border:0px; outline:0px; font-weight:inherit; font-style:inherit; font-family:inherit; vertical-align:baseline">
Spring:4.0.6</li></ul>
<p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:20px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; border:0px; outline:0px; font-weight:inherit; font-style:inherit; font-family:inherit; vertical-align:baseline; letter-spacing:0.01rem; line-height:2em">
本例子在我的这个环境中运行正常， 全部代码可以到 <a target="_blank" href="https://github.com/smallnest/spring-kafka-demo" rel="nofollow" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; border:0px; outline:0px; font-weight:inherit; font-style:inherit; font-family:inherit; vertical-align:baseline; text-decoration:none">github</a> 下载。<br>
<a target="_blank" id="more" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; border:0px; outline:0px; font-weight:inherit; font-style:inherit; font-family:inherit; vertical-align:baseline"></a></p>
<p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:20px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; border:0px; outline:0px; font-weight:inherit; font-style:inherit; font-family:inherit; vertical-align:baseline; letter-spacing:0.01rem; line-height:2em">
本文所有的操作系统用户都是<code style='margin:0px; padding:0px 0.3em; border:1px solid rgb(220,220,220); outline:0px; font-weight:inherit; font-style:inherit; font-family:Consolas,"Source Code Pro",Monaco,Menlo,Consolas,monospace,"Courier New"; font-size:0.85em; vertical-align:baseline; background:rgb(240,240,240)'>root</code>。
 实际产品中可能安全标准需要特定的用户如<code style='margin:0px; padding:0px 0.3em; border:1px solid rgb(220,220,220); outline:0px; font-weight:inherit; font-style:inherit; font-family:Consolas,"Source Code Pro",Monaco,Menlo,Consolas,monospace,"Courier New"; font-size:0.85em; vertical-align:baseline; background:rgb(240,240,240)'>zookeeper</code>, <code style='margin:0px; padding:0px 0.3em; border:1px solid rgb(220,220,220); outline:0px; font-weight:inherit; font-style:inherit; font-family:Consolas,"Source Code Pro",Monaco,Menlo,Consolas,monospace,"Courier New"; font-size:0.85em; vertical-align:baseline; background:rgb(240,240,240)'>kafka</code>等。</p>
<h2 id="安装Zookeeper" style='margin:2.2em 0px 1.1em; padding:0px 0px 5px; border-width:0px 0px 1px; border-top-style:initial; border-right-style:initial; border-bottom-style:solid; border-left-style:initial; border-top-color:initial; border-right-color:initial; border-bottom-color:rgb(204,204,204); border-left-color:initial; outline:0px; font-style:inherit; font-family:"Droid Serif","Segoe UI",Georgia,serif; font-size:1.6em; vertical-align:baseline; line-height:1.1em; counter-reset:section 0'>
安装Zookeeper</h2>
<p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:20px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; border:0px; outline:0px; font-weight:inherit; font-style:inherit; font-family:inherit; vertical-align:baseline; letter-spacing:0.01rem; line-height:2em">
首先下载解压zookeeper,选择合适的镜像站点以加快下载速度。<br>
我们可以将zookeeper加到系统服务中， 增加一个<code style='margin:0px; padding:0px 0.3em; border:1px solid rgb(220,220,220); outline:0px; font-weight:inherit; font-style:inherit; font-family:Consolas,"Source Code Pro",Monaco,Menlo,Consolas,monospace,"Courier New"; font-size:0.85em; vertical-align:baseline; background:rgb(240,240,240)'>/etc/init.d/zookeeper</code>文件。</p>

<p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:20px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; border:0px; outline:0px; font-weight:inherit; font-style:inherit; font-family:inherit; vertical-align:baseline; letter-spacing:0.01rem; line-height:2em">
将<a target="_blank" href="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/apache/zookeeper/trunk/src/packages/rpm/init.d/zookeeper" rel="nofollow" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; border:0px; outline:0px; font-weight:inherit; font-style:inherit; font-family:inherit; vertical-align:baseline; text-decoration:none">https://raw.githubusercontent.com/apache/zookeeper/trunk/src/packages/rpm/init.d/zookeeper</a>文件的内容拷贝到这个文件，修改其中的运行zookeeper的用户以及zookeeper的文件夹位置。</p>

<h2 id="安装Kafka" style='margin:2.2em 0px 1.1em; padding:0px 0px 5px; border-width:0px 0px 1px; border-top-style:initial; border-right-style:initial; border-bottom-style:solid; border-left-style:initial; border-top-color:initial; border-right-color:initial; border-bottom-color:rgb(204,204,204); border-left-color:initial; outline:0px; font-style:inherit; font-family:"Droid Serif","Segoe UI",Georgia,serif; font-size:1.6em; vertical-align:baseline; line-height:1.1em; counter-reset:section 0'>
安装Kafka</h2>
<p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:20px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; border:0px; outline:0px; font-weight:inherit; font-style:inherit; font-family:inherit; vertical-align:baseline; letter-spacing:0.01rem; line-height:2em">
从合适的镜像站点下载最新的kafka并解压。</p>
<table style="margin:0px; padding:0px; border:0px; outline:0px; font-weight:inherit; font-style:inherit; font-family:inherit; font-size:0.8em; vertical-align:middle; border-collapse:collapse; border-spacing:0px; max-width:100%; line-height:1.6em; width:auto">

<p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:20px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; border:0px; outline:0px; font-weight:inherit; font-style:inherit; font-family:inherit; vertical-align:baseline; letter-spacing:0.01rem; line-height:2em">
更多的介绍可以查看我翻译整理的 <a target="_blank" href="http://colobu.com/2014/08/06/kafka-quickstart/" rel="nofollow" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; border:0px; outline:0px; font-weight:inherit; font-style:inherit; font-family:inherit; vertical-align:baseline; text-decoration:none">Kafka快速入门</a></p>
<h2 id="创建一个Spring项目" style='margin:2.2em 0px 1.1em; padding:0px 0px 5px; border-width:0px 0px 1px; border-top-style:initial; border-right-style:initial; border-bottom-style:solid; border-left-style:initial; border-top-color:initial; border-right-color:initial; border-bottom-color:rgb(204,204,204); border-left-color:initial; outline:0px; font-style:inherit; font-family:"Droid Serif","Segoe UI",Georgia,serif; font-size:1.6em; vertical-align:baseline; line-height:1.1em; counter-reset:section 0'>
创建一个Spring项目</h2>
<p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:20px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; border:0px; outline:0px; font-weight:inherit; font-style:inherit; font-family:inherit; vertical-align:baseline; letter-spacing:0.01rem; line-height:2em">
以上的准备环境完成，让我们开始创建一个项目。<br>
以前我写过一篇简单介绍: <a target="_blank" href="http://colobu.com/2014/08/07/spring-integration-kafka/" rel="nofollow" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; border:0px; outline:0px; font-weight:inherit; font-style:inherit; font-family:inherit; vertical-align:baseline; text-decoration:none">Spring
 集成 Kafka</a>.<br>
<a target="_blank" href="https://github.com/spring-projects/spring-integration-kafka" rel="nofollow" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; border:0px; outline:0px; font-weight:inherit; font-style:inherit; font-family:inherit; vertical-align:baseline; text-decoration:none">spring-integration-kafka</a>这个官方框架我就不介绍了。
 我们主要使用它做集成。</p>
<p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:20px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; border:0px; outline:0px; font-weight:inherit; font-style:inherit; font-family:inherit; vertical-align:baseline; letter-spacing:0.01rem; line-height:2em">
首先我们先看一下使用Kafka自己的Producer/Consumer API发送/接收消息的例子。</p>
<h3 id="使用Producer_API发送消息到Kafka" style='margin:2.2em 0px 1.1em; padding:0px; border:0px; outline:0px; font-style:inherit; font-family:"Droid Serif","Segoe UI",Georgia,serif; font-size:1.4em; vertical-align:baseline; line-height:1.1em; counter-reset:subsection 0'>

这个例子中首先初始化Producer对象，指定相应的broker和serializer， 然后发送100个字符串消息给Kafka。</p>

<p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:20px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; border:0px; outline:0px; font-weight:inherit; font-style:inherit; font-family:inherit; vertical-align:baseline; letter-spacing:0.01rem; line-height:2em">
在生产者控制台输入几条消息，可以看到运行这个例子的控制台可以将这些消息打印出来。</p>
<p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:20px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; border:0px; outline:0px; font-weight:inherit; font-style:inherit; font-family:inherit; vertical-align:baseline; letter-spacing:0.01rem; line-height:2em">
教程的代码中还包括一个使用Simple Consumer API接收消息的例子。 因为spring-integration-kafka不支持这种API，这里也不列出对比代码了。</p>
<h3 id="使用spring-integration-kafka发送消息" style='margin:2.2em 0px 1.1em; padding:0px; border:0px; outline:0px; font-style:inherit; font-family:"Droid Serif","Segoe UI",Georgia,serif; font-size:1.4em; vertical-align:baseline; line-height:1.1em; counter-reset:subsection 0'>
使用spring-integration-kafka发送消息</h3>
<p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:20px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; border:0px; outline:0px; font-weight:inherit; font-style:inherit; font-family:inherit; vertical-align:baseline; letter-spacing:0.01rem; line-height:2em">
Outbound Channel Adapter用来发送消息到Kafka。 消息从Spring Integration Channel中读取。 你可以在Spring application context指定这个channel。<br>
一旦配置好这个Channel，就可以利用这个Channel往Kafka发消息。 明显地，Spring Integration特定的消息发送给这个Adaptor，然后发送前在内部被转为Kafka消息。当前的版本要求你必须指定消息key和topic作为头部数据 (header)，消息作为有载荷(payload)。<br>
例如</p>
<table style="margin:0px; padding:0px; border:0px; outline:0px; font-weight:inherit; font-style:inherit; font-family:inherit; font-size:0.8em; vertical-align:middle; border-collapse:collapse; border-spacing:0px; max-width:100%; line-height:1.6em; width:auto">
<tbody style="margin:0px; padding:0px; border:0px; outline:0px; font-weight:inherit; font-style:inherit; font-family:inherit; font-size:12.8px; vertical-align:baseline">

<td class="code" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; border:none; outline:0px; font-style:inherit; font-family:inherit; font-size:12.8px; vertical-align:middle">

<p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:20px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; border:0px; outline:0px; font-weight:inherit; font-style:inherit; font-family:inherit; vertical-align:baseline; letter-spacing:0.01rem; line-height:2em">

<pre style='margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding:0px 20px 0px 0px; border:none; outline:0px; font-weight:inherit; font-style:inherit; font-family:Consolas,"Source Code Pro",Monaco,Menlo,Consolas,monospace,"Courier New"; font-weight:inherit; font-style:inherit; font-family:inherit; vertical-align:baseline; height:25.6px">		} <span class="keyword" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; border:0px; outline:0px; font-weight:inherit; font-style:inherit; font-family:inherit; vertical-align:baseline">catch</span> (InterruptedException e) {</div><div class="line" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; border:0px; outline:0px; font-weight:inherit; font-style:inherit; font-family:inherit; vertical-align:baseline; height:25.6px">			e.printStackTrace();</div><div class="line" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; border:0px; outline:0px; font-weight:inherit; font-style:inherit; font-family:inherit; vertical-align:baseline; height:25.6px">		}</div><div class="line" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; border:0px; outline:0px; font-weight:inherit; font-style:inherit; font-family:inherit; vertical-align:baseline; height:25.6px">		ctx.close();</div><div class="line" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; border:0px; outline:0px; font-weight:inherit; font-style:inherit; font-family:inherit; vertical-align:baseline; height:25.6px">	}</div><div class="line" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; border:0px; outline:0px; font-weight:inherit; font-style:inherit; font-family:inherit; vertical-align:baseline; height:25.6px">}</div></pre>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

<p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:20px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; border:0px; outline:0px; font-weight:inherit; font-style:inherit; font-family:inherit; vertical-align:baseline; letter-spacing:0.01rem; line-height:2em">
<code style='margin:0px; padding:0px 0.3em; border:1px solid rgb(220,220,220); outline:0px; font-weight:inherit; font-style:inherit; font-family:Consolas,"Source Code Pro",Monaco,Menlo,Consolas,monospace,"Courier New"; font-size:0.85em; vertical-align:baseline; background:rgb(240,240,240)'>int:channel</code>是配置Spring
 Integration Channel, 此channel基于queue。<br>
<code style='margin:0px; padding:0px 0.3em; border:1px solid rgb(220,220,220); outline:0px; font-weight:inherit; font-style:inherit; font-family:Consolas,"Source Code Pro",Monaco,Menlo,Consolas,monospace,"Courier New"; font-size:0.85em; vertical-align:baseline; background:rgb(240,240,240)'>int-kafka:outbound-channel-adapter</code>是outbound-channel-adapter对象，
 内部使用一个线程池处理消息。关键是<code style='margin:0px; padding:0px 0.3em; border:1px solid rgb(220,220,220); outline:0px; font-weight:inherit; font-style:inherit; font-family:Consolas,"Source Code Pro",Monaco,Menlo,Consolas,monospace,"Courier New"; font-size:0.85em; vertical-align:baseline; background:rgb(240,240,240)'>kafka-producer-context-ref</code>。<br>
<code style='margin:0px; padding:0px 0.3em; border:1px solid rgb(220,220,220); outline:0px; font-weight:inherit; font-style:inherit; font-family:Consolas,"Source Code Pro",Monaco,Menlo,Consolas,monospace,"Courier New"; font-size:0.85em; vertical-align:baseline; background:rgb(240,240,240)'>int-kafka:producer-context</code>配置producer列表，要处理的topic，这些Producer最终要转换成Kafka的Producer。</p>
<p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:20px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; border:0px; outline:0px; font-weight:inherit; font-style:inherit; font-family:inherit; vertical-align:baseline; letter-spacing:0.01rem; line-height:2em">

font-weight:inherit; font-style:inherit; font-family:inherit; vertical-align:baseline">key</span> <span class="keyword" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; border:0px; outline:0px; font-weight:inherit; font-style:inherit; font-family:inherit; vertical-align:baseline">class</span>. This will be ignored <span class="keyword" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; border:0px; outline:0px; font-weight:inherit; font-style:inherit; font-family:inherit; vertical-align:baseline">if</span> no <span class="keyword" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; border:0px; outline:0px; font-weight:inherit; font-style:inherit; font-family:inherit; vertical-align:baseline">key</span>-encoder <span class="keyword" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; border:0px; outline:0px; font-weight:inherit; font-style:inherit; font-family:inherit; vertical-align:baseline">is</span> provided</div><div class="line" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; border:0px; outline:0px; font-weight:inherit; font-style:inherit; font-family:inherit; vertical-align:baseline; height:25.6px">value-<span class="keyword" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; border:0px; outline:0px; font-weight:inherit; font-style:inherit; font-family:inherit; vertical-align:baseline">class</span>-type        Type <span class="keyword" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; border:0px; outline:0px; font-weight:inherit; font-style:inherit; font-family:inherit; vertical-align:baseline">of</span> the value <span class="keyword" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; border:0px; outline:0px; font-weight:inherit; font-style:inherit; font-family:inherit; vertical-align:baseline">class</span>. This will be ignored <span class="keyword" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; border:0px; outline:0px; font-weight:inherit; font-style:inherit; font-family:inherit; vertical-align:baseline">if</span> no value-encoder <span class="keyword" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; border:0px; outline:0px; font-weight:inherit; font-style:inherit; font-family:inherit; vertical-align:baseline">is</span> provided.</div><div class="line" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; border:0px; outline:0px; font-weight:inherit; font-style:inherit; font-family:inherit; vertical-align:baseline; height:25.6px">partitioner             <span class="keyword" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; border:0px; outline:0px; font-weight:inherit; font-style:inherit; font-family:inherit; vertical-align:baseline">Custom</span> implementation <span class="keyword" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; border:0px; outline:0px; font-weight:inherit; font-style:inherit; font-family:inherit; vertical-align:baseline">of</span> a Kafka Partitioner <span class="keyword" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; border:0px; outline:0px; font-weight:inherit; font-style:inherit; font-family:inherit; vertical-align:baseline">interface</span>.</div><div class="line" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; border:0px; outline:0px; font-weight:inherit; font-style:inherit; font-family:inherit; vertical-align:baseline; height:25.6px">async                   <span class="literal" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; border:0px; outline:0px; font-weight:inherit; font-style:inherit; font-family:inherit; vertical-align:baseline">True</span>/<span class="literal" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; border:0px; outline:0px; font-weight:inherit; font-style:inherit; font-family:inherit; vertical-align:baseline">False</span> - <span class="keyword" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; border:0px; outline:0px; font-weight:inherit; font-style:inherit; font-family:inherit; vertical-align:baseline">default</span> <span class="keyword" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; border:0px; outline:0px; font-weight:inherit; font-style:inherit; font-family:inherit; vertical-align:baseline">is</span> <span class="literal" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; border:0px; outline:0px; font-weight:inherit; font-style:inherit; font-family:inherit; vertical-align:baseline">false</span>. Setting this <span class="keyword" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; border:0px; outline:0px; font-weight:inherit; font-style:inherit; font-family:inherit; vertical-align:baseline">to</span> <span class="literal" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; border:0px; outline:0px; font-weight:inherit; font-style:inherit; font-family:inherit; vertical-align:baseline">true</span> would make the Kafka producer <span class="keyword" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; border:0px; outline:0px; font-weight:inherit; font-style:inherit; font-family:inherit; vertical-align:baseline">to</span> use</div><div class="line" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; border:0px; outline:0px; font-weight:inherit; font-style:inherit; font-family:inherit; vertical-align:baseline; height:25.6px">                        an async producer</div><div class="line" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; border:0px; outline:0px; font-weight:inherit; font-style:inherit; font-family:inherit; vertical-align:baseline; height:25.6px">batch-num-messages      Number <span class="keyword" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; border:0px; outline:0px; font-weight:inherit; font-style:inherit; font-family:inherit; vertical-align:baseline">of</span> messages <span class="keyword" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; border:0px; outline:0px; font-weight:inherit; font-style:inherit; font-family:inherit; vertical-align:baseline">to</span> batch at the producer. <span class="keyword" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; border:0px; outline:0px; font-weight:inherit; font-style:inherit; font-family:inherit; vertical-align:baseline">If</span> async <span class="keyword" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; border:0px; outline:0px; font-weight:inherit; font-style:inherit; font-family:inherit; vertical-align:baseline">is</span> <span class="literal" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; border:0px; outline:0px; font-weight:inherit; font-style:inherit; font-family:inherit; vertical-align:baseline">false</span>, <span class="keyword" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; border:0px; outline:0px; font-weight:inherit; font-style:inherit; font-family:inherit; vertical-align:baseline">then</span> this has no effect.</div></pre>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:20px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; border:0px; outline:0px; font-weight:inherit; font-style:inherit; font-family:inherit; vertical-align:baseline; letter-spacing:0.01rem; line-height:2em">
value-encoder 和key-encoder可以是其它实现了Kafka Encoder接口的Bean。同样partitioner也是实现了Kafka的Partitioner接口的Bean。<br>

<p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:20px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; border:0px; outline:0px; font-weight:inherit; font-style:inherit; font-family:inherit; vertical-align:baseline; letter-spacing:0.01rem; line-height:2em">
Spring Integration Kafka 也提供了个基于Avro的Encoder。 <a target="_blank" href="http://avro.apache.org/" rel="nofollow" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; border:0px; outline:0px; font-weight:inherit; font-style:inherit; font-family:inherit; vertical-align:baseline; text-decoration:none">Avro</a>也是Apache的一个项目，
 在大数据处理时也是一个常用的序列化框架。<br>
不指定Encoder将使用Kafka缺省的Encoder (kafka.serializer.DefaultEncoder, byte[] --&gt; same byte[])。</p>
<p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:20px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; border:0px; outline:0px; font-weight:inherit; font-style:inherit; font-family:inherit; vertical-align:baseline; letter-spacing:0.01rem; line-height:2em">
<code style='margin:0px; padding:0px 0.3em; border:1px solid rgb(220,220,220); outline:0px; font-weight:inherit; font-style:inherit; font-family:Consolas,"Source Code Pro",Monaco,Menlo,Consolas,monospace,"Courier New"; font-size:0.85em; vertical-align:baseline; background:rgb(240,240,240)'>producerProperties</code>可以用来设置配置属性进行调优。配置属性列表请参考 <a target="_blank" href="http://kafka.apache.org/documentation.html#producerconfigs" rel="nofollow" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; border:0px; outline:0px; font-weight:inherit; font-style:inherit; font-family:inherit; vertical-align:baseline; text-decoration:none">http://kafka.apache.org/documentation.html#producerconfigs</a></p>

</tbody>
</table>
<p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:20px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; border:0px; outline:0px; font-weight:inherit; font-style:inherit; font-family:inherit; vertical-align:baseline; letter-spacing:0.01rem; line-height:2em">
这个配置和Producer类似， 同样声明一个channel, 定义<code style='margin:0px; padding:0px 0.3em; border:1px solid rgb(220,220,220); outline:0px; font-weight:inherit; font-style:inherit; font-family:Consolas,"Source Code Pro",Monaco,Menlo,Consolas,monospace,"Courier New"; font-size:0.85em; vertical-align:baseline; background:rgb(240,240,240)'>inbound-channel-adapter</code>,
 它引用Bean <code style='margin:0px; padding:0px 0.3em; border:1px solid rgb(220,220,220); outline:0px; font-weight:inherit; font-style:inherit; font-family:Consolas,"Source Code Pro",Monaco,Menlo,Consolas,monospace,"Courier New"; font-size:0.85em; vertical-align:baseline; background:rgb(240,240,240)'>kafka-consumer-context</code>,<br>
<code style='margin:0px; padding:0px 0.3em; border:1px solid rgb(220,220,220); outline:0px; font-weight:inherit; font-style:inherit; font-family:Consolas,"Source Code Pro",Monaco,Menlo,Consolas,monospace,"Courier New"; font-size:0.85em; vertical-align:baseline; background:rgb(240,240,240)'>kafka-consumer-context</code>定义了消费者的列表。 <code style='margin:0px; padding:0px 0.3em; border:1px solid rgb(220,220,220); outline:0px; font-weight:inherit; font-style:inherit; font-family:Consolas,"Source Code Pro",Monaco,Menlo,Consolas,monospace,"Courier New"; font-size:0.85em; vertical-align:baseline; background:rgb(240,240,240)'>consumer-configuration</code>还提供了<code style='margin:0px; padding:0px 0.3em; border:1px solid rgb(220,220,220); outline:0px; font-weight:inherit; font-style:inherit; font-family:Consolas,"Source Code Pro",Monaco,Menlo,Consolas,monospace,"Courier New"; font-size:0.85em; vertical-align:baseline; background:rgb(240,240,240)'>topic-filter</code>，使用正则表达式建立白名单或者黑名单(exclude属性)。</p>
<p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:20px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; border:0px; outline:0px; font-weight:inherit; font-style:inherit; font-family:inherit; vertical-align:baseline; letter-spacing:0.01rem; line-height:2em">
消费者上下文还需要<code style='margin:0px; padding:0px 0.3em; border:1px solid rgb(220,220,220); outline:0px; font-weight:inherit; font-style:inherit; font-family:Consolas,"Source Code Pro",Monaco,Menlo,Consolas,monospace,"Courier New"; font-size:0.85em; vertical-align:baseline; background:rgb(240,240,240)'>zookeeper-connect</code>。</p>
<p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:20px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; border:0px; outline:0px; font-weight:inherit; font-style:inherit; font-family:inherit; vertical-align:baseline; letter-spacing:0.01rem; line-height:2em">
由于spring-integration-kafka只实现了high level Consumer API,这也就意味着你不可能回滚重新查看以前的消息， 因为high level API不提供offset管理。</p>
<p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:20px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; border:0px; outline:0px; font-weight:inherit; font-style:inherit; font-family:inherit; vertical-align:baseline; letter-spacing:0.01rem; line-height:2em">
注意Channel中得到的有效负载的类型是：<br>
<code style='margin:0px; padding:0px 0.3em; border:1px solid rgb(220,220,220); outline:0px; font-weight:inherit; font-style:inherit; font-family:Consolas,"Source Code Pro",Monaco,Menlo,Consolas,monospace,"Courier New"; font-size:0.85em; vertical-align:baseline; background:rgb(240,240,240)'>Map&lt;String,
 Map&lt;Integer, List&lt;Object&gt;&gt;&gt;</code>,<br>
这个Map的key是topic, 值还是另外的Map对象。<br>
这个值Map的key值是分区号，value值是消息列表。 在本例中由于消息是字符串， 转换成了byte[]数组。</p>
<p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:20px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; border:0px; outline:0px; font-weight:inherit; font-style:inherit; font-family:inherit; vertical-align:baseline; letter-spacing:0.01rem; line-height:2em">
这种复杂的结构是由于Kafka的设计造成的。 Kafka保证对于同一个topic的同一个分区的消息是严格有序的。所有这种数据结构可以提供有序的消息。</p>
</div>
<br>
<p></p>
            </div>
                </div>
